<div><a name="s81CD73CA54462946516F5E8A625C526B"></a></div><div><div style="line-height:144%;text-align:right;font-size:9pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:9pt;"><br></font></div></div><div><br></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;"><img src="businessupdate_image1.jpg" alt="businessupdate_image1.jpg" style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;height:66px;width:66px;"></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">GE PROVIDES UPDATES ON GUIDANCE AND FIRST QUARTER</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:13px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:-2px;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">GE withdraws financial guidance due to uncertainty associated with COVID-19</font></div></td></tr></table><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:13px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:10pt;padding-left:-2px;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">Preliminary view of first-quarter results indicates adjusted EPS* materially below prior guidance of about $0.10; Industrial free cash flow* near the prior guidance of negative $2 billion</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">BOSTON - April 9, 2020 - GE (NYSE:GE) today provided an update on its financial guidance and first-quarter performance. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">Given the evolving nature of the COVID-19 pandemic, at this time, GE cannot forecast with reasonable accuracy the full duration, magnitude, and pace of recovery across our end markets, operations, and supply chains. Therefore, the Company believes it is prudent to withdraw guidance for 2020. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">For the first quarter ended March 31, 2020, GE preliminarily expects adjusted EPS* to be materially below its                                                              prior guidance of about $0.10, which the Company had shared on March 4, 2020. GE preliminarily expects Industrial free cash flow* to be near the prior guidance of about negative $2 billion. Total company adjusted EPS* deteriorated to a greater extent than Industrial free cash flow* primarily due to non-cash and timing items in Aviation, Renewable Energy, and GE Capital. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">GE Chairman and CEO H. Lawrence Culp, Jr., said, &#8220;We are taking swift actions across the company to position GE to come out stronger on the other side of the COVID-19 crisis. With net proceeds of about $20 billion from the BioPharma transaction now in hand, we have more flexibility to de-risk and further strengthen our balance sheet. We are committed to bringing down our leverage over time as we navigate this period of uncertainty and position ourselves for the future.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">GE remains focused on the safety of its employees, serving customers in their time of need, and preserving the Company&#8217;s strength. Each of GE&#8217;s businesses and Corporate are </font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;color:#0563c1;text-decoration:underline;">taking cost and cash actions</font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">&#32;to manage risk and proactively mitigate the financial impacts from COVID-19. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">Culp continued, &#8220;The entire GE team is proudly supporting those on the front lines across the globe, helping clinicians, communities, and the broader healthcare ecosystem combat COVID-19 while continuing to support and deliver critical infrastructure across our businesses. We will continue to rise to the challenge of helping our customers adapt through this time of uncertainty as well as the eventual recovery.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">GE plans to hold its first-quarter earnings call on Wednesday, April 29, 2020, at 8:00AM ET, where it will share additional details. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">For more on the Company&#8217;s efforts and contributions in the fight against COVID-19, visit GE Reports </font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;color:#0563c1;text-decoration:underline;">here</font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Caution Concerning Forward-Looking Statements</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">This document contains forward-looking statements - that is, statements related to future events that by their nature address matters that are, to different degrees, uncertain.  For details on the uncertainties that may cause our actual future results to be materially different than those expressed in our forward-looking statements, see </font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;color:#0563c1;text-decoration:underline;">https://www.ge.com/investor-relations/important-forward-looking-statement-information</font><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">, as well as our annual report on Form 10-K. We do not undertake to update our forward-looking statements.  </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Non-GAAP Financial Measures</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:GE Inspira Sans,sans-serif;font-size:10pt;">We sometimes use information derived from consolidated financial data but not presented in our financial statements prepared in accordance with U.S. generally accepted accounting principles (GAAP).
